msg:The area around the hotel is a bit desolate and lacks supporting facilities for life, but the hotel itself is located in a large area with ample parking spaces. The lobby is decorated in a magnificent style, and there are many valuable wooden artworks. This hotel was invested and founded by a local enterprise in Nanjing. Next to the hotel is the heavy machinery factory affiliated with this enterprise, and the light rail subway is also next to it. Overall, this hotel has a rich breakfast, complete facilities, and a comfortable stay. Deputy Manager Cao in the lobby is professionally trained, and the service is polite, thoughtful and enthusiastic. Fruits were also sent.

I would like to mention a few shortcomings. First, the hygiene details of the guest rooms need to be paid more attention. The floating dust on them is quite thick. Refer to the last two photos. msg:Due to thunderstorms in Guangzhou at the end of April, we were originally scheduled to fly from Nanjing to Guangzhou on Friday night. After going through 3 airlines and 6 flights, we finally flew back to Guangzhou successfully on Monday afternoon.

During this period, Shenzhen Airlines took us to Xipu Hotel, which is about half an hour away from the airport.

It was unexpectedly good, because: clean, the bedding is soft and hard, the shower water is big, and the price is more surprising, it is only more than 300 yuan.

And the next day, because I lost the charging cable, I charged it with a power bank for more than 40 yuan because I was afraid of delaying the flight. The front desk also gave me a multi-head charging cable.

I stayed for two consecutive nights (one night for Shenzhen Airlines and one night for myself)

Except that the location is not particularly convenient, the other is fast price, four-star quality
